commit 1c0b2b2f62b217c84394f01f9b2b4f157391ded6
Author: Yanovsky, Daniel <daniel.yanovsky@intel.com>
Date:   Thu Mar 2 20:12:48 2017 +0200

    New module params for changing DG/CVE NR/LLC configuration
    =========================================================
    
    This param allows the user to select driver’s configuration
    (DG/CVE NR/LLC) according to predefined set:
    
    0=Default Configuration
    1=SINGLE_DEVICE_PER_GROUP - Many CVE configuration
    2=SINGLE_GROUP_ALL_DEVICES
    3=SINGLE_GROUP_SINGLE_DEVICE - Single CVE configuration *
    
    * For Single CVE configuration you can select specific CVE device by
    using "select_cve_dev_id" param.
    
    Usage (in Simics)
    modprobe intel_cve
    modprobe intel_cve driver_dg_settings=1
    modprobe intel_cve driver_dg_settings=2
    modprobe intel_cve driver_dg_settings=3 select_cve_dev_id=5
    
    Tested on Simics/Ring3
    
    Change-Id: I432e465a42f7156c0a9caa3552472ba41e9c2f9a

commit 59379aa407e56eeb9f0dc6128f2a7b865af1aea9
Author: Yanovsky, Daniel <daniel.yanovsky@intel.com>
Date:   Thu Mar 2 15:33:35 2017 +0200

    Many CVE - milestone 3: Many CVE enablement!
    
    This commit is the final stage of Many CVE feature.
    Many CVE is supported by the driver now.
    
    What's new:
    1. DG is selected in WQ creation (can be disabled by
       enabling DISABLE_DG_SELECTION_PER_WQ in dispatcher.c)
    2. User Buffers are mapped to all CVE devices per context
    3. Base FWs are mapped to all CVE devices per context
    4. Custom FWs are loaded & mapped per CVE device per context
    5. FIFO is allocated and mapped per CVE device per context
    
    Tested on Ring3/FPGA/Simics.
    Tested with leak detector on Ring3 when many CVE enabled
    (setenv CVE_DG_CONFIG 1)
    Tested with leak detector on FPGA
    PASS ALL driver's tests on Simics
    
    Change-Id: I33d6ab455937574341c219df3c3a6b817507e271

commit 011f929143f831dba11b9fe4b2e36ab6a7b83bf7
Author: Atedgi, Liron <liron.atedgi@intel.com>
Date:   Mon Jan 9 11:44:14 2017 +0200

    Adding jobgroup dependencies
    
    Each jobgroup can have dependencies of other
    jobgroups which reside in the same workqueue.
    Upon jobgroup submission a dependency list is
    created, each refcounter of the jobgroups in the
    dependency list is being incremented. On Jobgroup
    completion, the dependency list is scanned and the
    refcounter is being decremented for each of its dependency,
    and for the completed jobgroup. When counter of jobgroup
    reach 0 the jobgroup destroyed (initilize to 1 upon creation).
    
    Change-Id: I05ccc15d94fc8c625e0f4511da367d15f0cdda26

commit f40ed719adeab71282948c3c38cc9bdd4b2027d1

commit 80e64ed9aca6b4169661645d87bf16be5bb5618e
Author: Skidanov, Alexey <alexey.skidanov@intel.com>
Date:   Thu Jan 5 15:19:10 2017 +0200

    Enable/Disable HW counters through debugfs
    
    The following  debugfs structure will be created per CVE:
        cve_<N>
         |--- enable_hw_counters
    
    The read the value:
        cat /sys/kernel/debug/cve_<N>/enable_hw_counters
    
    The change the value:
        echo 0 > /sys/kernel/debug/cve_<N>/enable_hw_counters
        echo 1 > /sys/kernel/debug/cve_<N>/enable_hw_counters

commit dfc796e3ead52dc79094a327a75160cf254ab578
Author: Atedgi, Liron <liron.atedgi@intel.com>
Date:   Wed Jan 4 15:04:26 2017 +0200

    Device group configuration
    
    Expose module params to set device group configuration.
    
    There are 2 array params which control the device group configurations:
    1. dg_devices_array - specify # of CVE devices in each DG
    2. dg_llc_array - specify llc size in each DG
    
    if no params specified the default configuration is taken e.g.:
    - insmod intel_cve.ko
    
    Few examples:
    
    CoH - 1 device group with 8 devices all 8MB LLC
    - intel_cve.ko dg_devices_array=8 dg_llc_array=8388608
    
    CoH - 2 device groups 3,5 devices 2MB and 6MB LLC
    - intel_cve.ko dg_devices_array=3,5 dg_llc_array=2097152,6291456
    
    CVE2 | CVE1 FPGA
    - intel_cve.ko dg_devices_array=1 dg_llc_array=0
    
    Change-Id: I5b6e8f3d066231d060dc89af969efd0331cec1db

commit 2eb561781d503397aad7a88f8edceb07c75e3e7d
Author: Skidanov, Alexey <alexey.skidanov@intel.com>
Date:   Mon Jan 2 15:32:22 2017 +0200

    Create debugfs directory per CVE
    
    Preparation for reading registers through debugfs. The following
    debugfs structure will be created per CVE:
    cve_<N>
     |--- registers
    
    The registers value may be read by:
    cat /sys/kernel/debug/cve_<N>/registers
    
    Change-Id: I1228a97dffc50b06d68de9bddd7a46c492394ff1

commit 6ccf2b88abbef525bc9e48e1291ce5c55b8cd156
Author: Atedgi, Liron <liron.atedgi@intel.com>
Date:   Sun Dec 25 15:31:13 2016 +0200

    Scheduler preparation
    
    1. Add basic scheduler support.
    2. Hold 3 WQ lists {IDLE, READY, DISPATCH}
    3. The union of the 3 WQ lists
    contain all the DG WQs, the intersection of
    the 3 lists is empty
    4. The scheduler logic will go in a round-robin
    manner on the READY WQs. After selecting a READY WQ
    it will try to dispatch a full JobGroup on the
    CVEs in the DG, if there are remaining CVEs
    in the DG that are still idle it will get
    the next READY WQ and continue to dispatch from it.
    
    Change-Id: I06a1f252035adb5481b0912b568c4881f4fc1357

Author: Dassa, Asaf <asaf.dassa@intel.com>
Date:   Wed Dec 7 11:39:56 2016 +0200

    Change DMA SG allocation algorithm to allocate chunks of contig pages
    
    This is the last milestone in moving to use non-contig DMA allocations.
    The new algorithm allocates chunks of contig pages on a greedy way.
    It tries to allocate as much as it can and prepare SGT with the list of pages.
    
    This commit was tested on FPGA CVE1, FPGA CVE2 and CoH simics with UMD #59006a491352a8caa52e9ee4297aa696f65f02ac

commit e9ac50bca5e2ed249f048ae443fd0b67aefa295a
Author: Atedgi, Liron <liron.atedgi@intel.com>
Date:   Tue Oct 18 15:22:36 2016 +0300

    fix DMA address rounding functions
    
    Functions round_{up|down}_cve_pagesize operates with cve_dma_addr_t
    that is essentially DMA address, and differs in size with
    pointer (like void*). On COH platform, void* is 32 bit while
    dma_addr_t is 64 bit. Thus, upper bits get lost in rounding, this leads
    to wrong memory address after rounding.
    
    Use macro preprocessor to properly handle the round up|down.
    
    Change-Id: If3531d57e24f39b177ac4981ca9c3cd95eed9317

commit 5b61e26d246817db601c25dcf6116e45395d9e67
Author: Yanovsky, Daniel <daniel.yanovsky@intel.com>
Date:   Wed Jul 27 12:54:13 2016 +0300

    Sleep while PUNIT change freq
    =============================
    
    After Punit gets the request, the worst case time for punit to complete
    frequency change by clearing the FREQVALID bit is 1 to 1.1 ms.
    This is because Punit may be in the middle of a different flow,
    and punit’s periodic task runs every 1ms to check for new requests.
    
    Change-Id: Ieb12d72c191a9ca28c4b056bff686bd17cc461d9

commit 5506b6bd504d6e155359de7dc9818a4e3265b910
Author: Vladimir Kondratiev <vladimir.kondratiev@intel.com>
Date:   Sun Jul 3 15:42:58 2016 +0300

    fix CVE MMU handling when OS and CVE page size differs
    
    Always cove whole OS page in CVE MMU; for this,
    calculate number of CVE pages based on OS pages number.
    
    Failing to do so results in dis-balance between pages allocation
    and free. When freeing, code always calculates number of CVE pages
    based on OS pages number.
    
    Change-Id: I1fb3c3c7fccd2d353b8b5a76e3607d9004a22897
    Signed-off-by: Vladimir Kondratiev <vladimir.kondratiev@intel.com>

Author: Vladimir Kondratiev <vladimir.kondratiev@intel.com>
Date:   Wed May 25 15:52:43 2016 +0300

    fix unaligned access when copying data to user
    
    When copying data to user, unaligned pointer provided by the user space
    in IOCTL data. put_user assumes pointer is aligned and does not
    compensate for unaligned transaction.
    
    Use copy_to_user instead; it handles all alignment issues.
    
    Change-Id: I56ded14b23060acff0f5c80a17b850b74a60d770
    Signed-off-by: Vladimir Kondratiev <vladimir.kondratiev@intel.com>

commit 41379e77cd6c4fb8a87b3d8820c05dd804011c69
Author: selbling <shirley.elbling@intel.com>
Date:   Thu Mar 31 10:13:29 2016 +0300

    a bug fixes :
    1)embedded command buffer was not added to a dispached job.
    2)UMD status field of pTaskImpl variable was not cleared upon destroy task.
    
    Analysis :
    1)embedded command buffer was added during reset handling . to current context
    JOB list , embedded command buffer should be added in do_dispatch() routine
    where a new job is dispatched , in case a reset was triggered.
    2)running validation test simulator_vx_intel_test_conformance --global_context=1 ,
    a page fault was triggered due to unmapping of surfaces. the root cause : UMD didn't
    block RT upon wait API , and signaled JOB completion instead therefore buffers where destroyed
    before JOB dispatched.
    
    Change-Id: Id088adf18b7f13abd238108dfa5db4b8134afd96

commit b40b24c869d2a71b1f3258ee4c69f6afc9b70c9b
Author: Atedgi, Liron <liron.atedgi@intel.com>
Date:   Mon Dec 21 16:19:07 2015 +0200

    The following change enable to maintain the surface mapping
    as part of the context, instead of per submission.
    The change involve both UMD & KMD.
    On buffer creation the memory will be pinned, be accessible to the
    device and will be added to the context page table.
    The destroy buffer API which is a blocking API, will unpin the memory
    and remove it from the context page table.
    
    Change-Id: I2b797fe09f1713feac6e0a32c8fd0adb274e0f28

    initialize fifo descriptors on dispatch
    
    This change is the 1st part of a series of upcoming changes, in order to
    to support mapping upon surface creation.
    The following changes include:
    1. detach context dependency between submission to dispatching, meaning
    alliocation of FIFO descriptors will be upon dispatching.
    All command buffer data will be associated with a subjob.

    3. FIX BUG of memmove code upon context switch
